<figure class="wp-block-image size-large is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="1024" src="https://fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1-1024x1024.png" alt="" class="wp-image-47528" style="width:216px;height:auto" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=1024%2C1024&amp;ssl=1 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=300%2C300&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=150%2C150&amp;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=768%2C768&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=1536%2C1536&amp;ssl=1 1536w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=500%2C500&amp;ssl=1 500w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=64%2C64&amp;ssl=1 64w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=600%2C600&amp;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=100%2C100&amp;ssl=1 100w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?resize=96%2C96&amp;ssl=1 96w, https://i0.wp.com/fitbutfun.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/CKS-1.png?w=1890&amp;ssl=1 1890w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure>
</li><li id="block-5" class="widget widget_block widget_text">
<p><br>Hey there, thanks for stopping by! </p>
</li><li id="block-8" class="widget widget_block widget_text">
<p>I'm Christine, I'm a working mom with a commute and two busy kids, so we need things that are <em>fast</em>! Meals we can cook in a hurry aren't always the healthiest but I try to sneak in nutrition where I can. A lot of the meals you find here at Fit But Fun won't be new, but I hope you find this site to be a great place to help simplify your meal planning!</p>
</li><li id="block-13" class="widget widget_block">

April is done and dusted, and life is flying by at warp speed. 😬

1. It was the peak of comp season, the girls grew a ton learning new styles of dance this year, brought home some hardware, and made so many memories.
2. It’s also high school baseball season. This team is so fun to watch! (Why are our kids activities in the exact same season? 😵‍💫) 
3. Visited the tulip festival with my bestie. 🌷
4. I have been talking a lot about freelance work lately, but that’s because I like helping moms find flex work. My job is still working with builders and interior designers!
5. Celebrated Easter. 🙏🏽✝️
6. 23 minute workouts are saving my life these days.
7. Meal prepping when I can! 
8. Prom: the final school dance for G.
9. Going through hundreds of pics and memories as we get ready for graduation in just a few weeks.

So much going on, there’s a lot of emotion and excitement in store for May. Looking forward to it but also trying to enjoy every moment! 💜

{"prefetch":[{"source":"document","where":{"and":[{"href_matches":"/*"},{"not":{"href_matches":["/wp-*.php","/wp-admin/*","/wp-content/uploads/*","/wp-content/*","/wp-content/plugins/*","/wp-content/themes/savor/*","/*\\?(.+)"]}},{"not":{"selector_matches":"a[rel~=\"nofollow\"]"}},{"not":{"selector_matches":".no-prefetch, .no-prefetch a"}}]},"eagerness":"conservative"}]}

		<script id="wppl-precheck-remember-me">
		(function() {
			'use strict';
			
			var wppl_precheck_remember_me = function() {
				var rememberMeNames = ["rememberme","remember","rcp_user_remember"];
				var processedElements = new Set(); // Track processed elements to avoid duplicates
				
				/**
				 * Check/enable a checkbox element
				 */
				function checkElement(element) {
					if (processedElements.has(element)) return;
					processedElements.add(element);
					
					if (element.type === 'checkbox' && !element.checked) {
						element.checked = true;
					}
				}
				
				/**
				 * Process standard remember me inputs
				 */
				function processRememberMeElements() {
					rememberMeNames.forEach(function(inputName) {
						// Find inputs by exact name match
						var inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="' + inputName + '"]');
						inputs.forEach(function(input) {
							checkElement(input);
						});
						
						// Also find inputs where name contains the input name (partial match)
						var partialInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
						partialInputs.forEach(function(input) {
							if (input.name && input.name.includes(inputName)) {
								checkElement(input);
							}
						});
					});
				}
				
				/**
				 * Handle WooCommerce specific elements
				 */
				function processWooCommerce() {
					var wooInputs = document.querySelectorAll('.woocommerce-form-login__rememberme input[type="checkbox"]');
					wooInputs.forEach(function(input) {
						checkElement(input);
					});
				}
				
				/**
				 * Handle Ultimate Member Plugin
				 */
				function processUltimateMember() {
					var umCheckboxLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.um-field-checkbox');
					
					umCheckboxLabels.forEach(function(label) {
						var input = label.querySelector('input');
						if (input && rememberMeNames.includes(input.name)) {
							// Set as active and checked
							checkElement(input);
							label.classList.add('active');
							
							// Update icon classes
							var icon = label.querySelector('.um-icon-android-checkbox-outline-blank');
							if (icon) {
								icon.classList.add('um-icon-android-checkbox-outline');
								icon.classList.remove('um-icon-android-checkbox-outline-blank');
							}
						}
					});
				}
				
				/**
				 * Handle ARMember Forms
				 */
				function processARMember() {
					var armContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.arm_form_input_container_rememberme');
					
					armContainers.forEach(function(container) {
						var checkboxes = container.querySelectorAll('md-checkbox');
						
						checkboxes.forEach(function(checkbox) {
							if (checkbox.classList.contains('ng-empty')) {
								checkbox.click(); // Activate the checkbox
							}
						});
					});
				}
				
				// Execute all processing functions
				processRememberMeElements();
				processWooCommerce();
				processUltimateMember();
				processARMember();
			};
			
			// Run when DOM is ready
			if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
				document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', wppl_precheck_remember_me);
			} else {
				wppl_precheck_remember_me();
			}
			
			// Also run after a short delay to catch dynamically loaded forms
			setTimeout(wppl_precheck_remember_me, 500);
			
		})();
		</script>
